	reestablish_the_state_of_baja = {
		##Reform a State from Nevada's territory
		cost = 100
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			AND = {
                original_tag = ERB
            }
		}
		visible = {

					country_exists = HIH
				}

						has_full_control_of_state = 866
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {

					has_completed_focus = enc_home_is_nevada
					OR = {
